msg:Let me talk about my experience. When I checked in in the evening, the hotel arranged a double bed room. After getting the room card, I was going to put down my luggage and go to eat. When it was found at the door of the room that the room card could not be swiped to open the door, they communicated through the telephone on the floor, and the hotel arranged for staff to make a new card and come to open the door. After the staff opened the door, I found that there were traces of staying in the hotel. Because I just wanted to put my luggage and didn't turn on the light, I asked the staff who came to open the door to confirm. After a closer look, it was found that there should be guests still staying, and they were obviously of the opposite sex. So I quickly exited and negotiated with the staff back to the front desk. The front desk staff arranged to change the room and upgrade the room type. In the evening, I went back to the hotel after dinner and took a rest. During the period, some staff members came to ask for an explanation and apologized, because they did not open the door to communicate because they were already asleep. Later, I thought about it, if I went out to eat without putting my luggage at that time, would it be on the social news when I went back to the hotel room? The hotel is now managed by the system. It is not understandable that such a problem occurs. The staff have a good attitude and actively deal with the problem, but I still think the hotel should not do it.
The next morning, I got the slippers wet after washing, and found that there was no other pair of slippers, only an empty plastic bag, and the bottle of body soap was also empty when I took a shower. I called and replaced it in time. Check out, because the mineral water in the room was not brought down, and the front desk proposed to bring a bottle of water before leaving, and told the concierge desk to get it. The concierge service staff even said that the water was gone, and asked the staff to return to the room, but they had already checked out. After negotiating with the front desk staff, the concierge went to fetch water. I communicated with friends in the same industry, saying that the big bed is made of two single beds, and it collapsed when sleeping in the middle.
The evaluation is not good. The experience of this stay is very strange.
May be management confusion during hotel brand switching? The quality of the staff is also uneven. A bad stay experience!
